      if (isAbort || !script.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test(script.readyState)) {
        script.onload = null;

    <p class="+type-body-two">
     Bankrate follows a strict editorial policy, so you can trust that were putting your interests first. Our award-winning editors and reporters create honest and accurate content to help you make the right financial decisions.
    </p>
    <h3 class="+type-heading-four +mg-bottom">
     Key Principles
    </h3>
    <p class="+type-body-two">
     We value your trust. Our mission is to provide readers with accurate and unbiased information, and we have editorial standards in place to ensure that happens. Our editors and reporters thoroughly fact-check editorial content to ensure the information youre reading is accurate. We maintain a firewall between our advertisers and our editorial team. Our editorial team does not receive direct compensation from our advertisers.
    </p>
    <h3 class="+type-heading-four +mg-bottom">
     Editorial Independence
    </h3>
    <p class="+type-body-two">
     Bankrates editorial team writes on behalf of YOU  the reader. Our goal is to give you the best advice to help you make smart personal finance decisions. We follow strict guidelines to ensure that our editorial content is not influenced by advertisers. Our editorial team receives no direct compensation from advertisers, and our content is thoroughly fact-checked to ensure accuracy. So, whether youre reading an article or a review, you can trust that youre getting credible and dependable information.
    </p>

  <script>
   ;(function () {
  function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + '='
    var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie)
    var ca = decodedCookie.split(';')
    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      var c = ca[i]
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
        c = c.substring(1)
      }
      if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
        return c.substring(name.length, c.length)
      }
    }
    return ''
  }

  function cookieToObj(cookie) {
    if (!cookie.length) {
      return {}
    }

    cookie = decodeURIComponent(cookie)

    try {
      cookie = JSON.parse(cookie)
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('failed to convert cookie to object')
    }

    return cookie
  }

  function hasPaidQueryParams() {
    const queryParams = window.location.search
    const hasCPC = queryParams.includes('utm_medium=cpc')
    const hasGoogle = queryParams.includes('utm_source=google')
    const hasBing = queryParams.includes('utm_source=bing')

    if (hasCPC && (hasGoogle || hasBing)) {
      return true
    }

    return false
  }

  function hasPaidCookie() {
    const attrCookie = getCookie('attr')
    const attrObj = cookieToObj(attrCookie)

    try {
      if (attrObj.utm_medium === 'cpc' && (attrObj.utm_source === 'google' || attrObj.utm_source === 'bing')) {
        return true
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('failed to read attr cookie')
    }

    return false
  }

  function isPaidTraffic() {
    return hasPaidQueryParams() || hasPaidCookie()
  }

  function swapLinks(findLink, swapLink) {
    const links = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(`[href*="${findLink}"]`))

    links.forEach((link) => {
      const href = link.getAttribute('href')
      let hrefQueryHash = href.match(/(\?|\#).*$/g)

      if (hrefQueryHash && hrefQueryHash.length) {
        hrefQueryHash = hrefQueryHash[0]

        if (/\?/.test(swapLink)) {
          hrefQueryHash = hrefQueryHash.replace('?', '&')
        }

        swapLink = `${swapLink}${hrefQueryHash}`
      }

      link.setAttribute('href', swapLink)
    })
  }

  if (isPaidTraffic()) {
    swapLinks(
      '/mortgages/mortgage-rates/',
      '/mortgages/landing-mortgage-rates/?mortgageType=Purchase'
    )

    swapLinks(
      '/mortgages/refinance-rates/',
      '/mortgages/landing-mortgage-rates/?mortgageType=Refinance'
    )
  }
})()
  </script>
